EventTargetChainItem.\n   */\n  uint16_t mItemFlags;\n\n  /**\n   * Data for items in the event target chain.\n   * Set in GetEventTargetParent() and used in PostHandleEvent().\n   *\n   * @note This data is different for each item in the event target chain.\n   *       It is up to the Pre/PostHandleEvent implementation to decide how to\n   *       use this.\n   */\n  nsCOMPtr<nsISupports> algorithm. The dispatch chain consists of five key components:\\n\\n## 1. Event Creation (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h/cpp, dom/events/Event.h/cpp)\\nThe process begins in `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:869), which is the main entry point for event dispatch. If needed, `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h:380) creates a DOM Event object from a WidgetEvent. The Event class (dom/events/Event.cpp) represents the public DOM event interface and stores event properties like type, target, phase, and timestamp.\\n\\n## 2. Event Target Identification (dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp, dom/base/nsIContent.h)\\nThe event target chain is built by calling `GetEventTargetParent()` on each target in the hierarchy. The base implementation is in `nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent()` (dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp:799), which determines:\\n  - Whether the current content can handle the event (mCanHandle flag)\\n  - The parent target for propagation (shadow DOM slots, normal parent, or null)\\n  - Event retargeting requirements across shadow DOM boundaries\\n  - Special handling for mouseover/mouseout and pointer events with related targets\\n\\nElement-specific implementations exist in dom/base/Element.cpp for link handling via `Element::GetEventTargetParentForLinks()` (dom/base/Element.cpp:4217).\\n\\n## 3. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp)\\nOnce the event target chain is built, `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:299) executes the three phases:\\n  - **Capture Phase** (lines 516-585): Iterates from root to target, checking mInCapturePhase flag, calling listeners with capture=true\\n  - **Target Phase** (lines 587-611): Dispatches to the actual event target (eMouseUp, eMouseDown, eClick, etc.) with both capture and bubbling listeners\\n  - **Bubble Phase** (lines 613-648): Iterates from target back to root if mBubbles is true, calling bubbling listeners\\n\\nThe EventChainPreVisitor and EventChainPostVisitor classes (dom/events/EventDispatcher.h:53-323) manage phase state, propagation flags, and event retargeting information throughout dispatch.\\n\\n## 4. Event Listener Invocation (dom/events/EventListenerManager.h/cpp, dom/events/EventTarget.cpp)\\nFor each event target in the chain, `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent()` (dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp:339) retrieves the EventListenerManager and calls its `HandleEvent()` method (dom/events/EventListenerManager.h:435). The system group dispatch (lines 651-693 in EventDispatcher.cpp) allows system code to perform default actions after content listeners have run.\\n\\n## Complete Dispatch Sequence\\n1. EventDispatcher::Dispatch() called with target and WidgetEvent\\n2. Event target chain built via GetEventTargetParent() traversal\\n3. EventChainPreVisitor set up with initial event state\\n4. Event Target Identification** (`dom/base/FragmentOrElement.cpp`, `dom/base/nsIContent.h`)\n- `nsIContent::GetEventTargetParent()` builds the event target chain\n- Handles event retargeting across shadow DOM boundaries\n- Determines propagation path through parent targets\n\n**3. Capture/Bubble Phase Traversal** (`dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp`)\n- `EventTargetChainItem::HandleEventTargetChain()` executes three phases:\n  - **Capture Phase**: Root to target (for capture listeners)\n  - **Target Phase**: The actual event target\n  - **Bubble Phase**: Target back to root (for bubble listeners)\n\n**4. Event Listener Invocation** (`dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp/h`, `dom/events/EventTarget.cpp`)\n- `EventListenerManager::HandleEvent()` invokes registered listeners\n- Handles both WebIDL callbacks and XPCOM interfaces\n- Respects capture/bubble phase, passive listeners, and \"once\" listeners\n\n**5.
